ACTOR SakuyaJackTheLudoBile
{
//$Category "Touhou Characters"
  Tag "Sakuya Izayoi"
  floatspeed 10
  Speed 10
  fastspeed 12
  MONSTER
  Health 1750
  Radius 24
  Height 64
  Scale 0.7
  MinMissileChance 64
  Mass 7000
  Species SDM
  +MISSILEMORE
  +MISSILEEVENMORE
  +INVULNERABLE
  +NOPAIN
  +DONTHURTSPECIES
  +AVOIDMELEE
  +LOOKALLAROUND
  +FLOORCLIP
  +NOTIMEFREEZE
  +DONTFALL
  +DONTRIP
  +DONTMORPH
  +NORADIUSDMG
  +AMBUSH
  +NOICEDEATH
  +BOSS
  Painchance 4
  Painsound "touhou/pain"
  Deathsound "touhou/nuefire"
  Obituary "%o was knived by Sakuya."
  DropItem "SakuyaNS2"
  States
  {
  Spawn:
	SAKU A 0
	SAKU A 15 A_SetTranslucent(0.1,0)
	SAKU AAAAAAAAAA 2 A_FadeIn(0.1)
  Idle:
	SAKU A 3 A_Look
    Loop
  See:
    SAKU A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("SpellcardActive",1,"ChaseState")
    SAKU A 0 A_GiveInventory("SpellcardActive",1)
	SAKU B 6 A_FaceTarget
    TNT1 A 0 Thing_ChangeTID(0,6036)
    TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecute("BHI_BossStartAttack",0,6036,2,true)
	TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecute("BHI_BossStartTimer",0,6036,60)
	SAKU B 0 ACS_Execute(602,0,22)
	SAKU B 0 A_PlaySound("touhou/spellcard",0,1,0,ATTN_NONE)
	SAKU CDEDE 6 A_FaceTarget
	SAKU A 0 A_UnSetInvulnerable
	SAKU A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOPAIN",0)
	Goto Missile
  ChaseState:
	SAKU A 0 A_UnSetInvulnerable
    SAKU A 3 A_Chase
	SAKU A 0 A_TakeInventory("EnemyCounter3",1)
    Loop
  Pain:
    SAKU S 5 A_Pain
    Goto See
  Melee:
  Missile:
	SAKU A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("EnemyCounter3",1,"See")
	SAKU A 0 A_GiveInventory("EnemyCounter3",50)
	SAKU A 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("EasyMode",1,"MissileEasy")
	SAKU A 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("NormalMode",1,"MissileNormal")
	SAKU A 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("HardMode",1,"MissileHard")
	SAKU A 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("LunaticMode",1,"MissileLunatic")
	Goto MissileHard
  MissileEasy:
	SAKU A 0 A_ChangeFlag("FRIGHTENED",1)
	SAKU A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOPAIN",1)
	SAKU LMNO 5 A_FaceTarget
	SAKU PPPPPPPPPPPPPPPPPPPPPPPPPPPPPPPPPPPPPPPPPPPPPPPPPPPPPPPPPPPP 0 A_CustomMissile("SakuyaClockCorpseOrb",32,0,frandom(90,-90),CMF_OFFSETPITCH,frandom(10,-10))
	SAKU PQRLMN 5 A_FaceTarget
	SAKU O 0 A_PlaySound("touhou/charge",0,1.0,0,ATTN_NONE)
	SAKU O 0 A_GiveInventory("SakuyaTimeFreeze",1) //OH GOD HERE WE GO
  EasyLoop:
	SAKU O 0 A_GiveInventory("EnemyCounter4")
	SAKU O 0 A_JumpIfInventory("EnemyCounter4",25,"MissileEnd")
	SAKU OOOOOOOOOO 0 A_Chase("","")
	SAKU OOOOOOOOOO 0 A_Wander
	SAKU O 0 A_PlaySound("touhou/fire")
	SAKU O 0 A_CustomMissile("SakuyaKnife1",32,-256,0)
	SAKU O 0 A_CustomMissile("SakuyaKnife1",32,-128,0)
	SAKU O 0 A_CustomMissile("SakuyaKnife1",32,128,0)
	SAKU O 0 A_CustomMissile("SakuyaKnife1",32,256,0)
	SAKU O 6 A_CustomMissile("SakuyaKnife1",32,0,0)
	Loop
  MissileNormal:
	SAKU A 0 A_ChangeFlag("FRIGHTENED",1)
	SAKU A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOPAIN",1)
	SAKU LMNO 5 A_FaceTarget
	SAKU PPPPPPPPPPPPPPPPPPPPPPPPPPPPPPPPPPPPPPPPPPPPPPPPPPPPPPPPPPPPPPPPPPPPPPPPPPPPPPPP 0 A_CustomMissile("SakuyaClockCorpseOrb",32,0,frandom(90,-90),CMF_OFFSETPITCH,frandom(10,-10))
	SAKU PQRLMN 5 A_FaceTarget
	SAKU O 0 A_PlaySound("touhou/charge",0,1.0,0,ATTN_NONE)
	SAKU O 0 A_GiveInventory("SakuyaTimeFreeze",1) //OH GOD HERE WE GO
  NormalLoop:
	SAKU O 0 A_GiveInventory("EnemyCounter4")
	SAKU O 0 A_JumpIfInventory("EnemyCounter4",25,"MissileEnd")
	SAKU OOOOOOOOOO 0 A_Chase("","")
	SAKU OOOOOOOOOO 0 A_Wander
	SAKU O 0 A_PlaySound("touhou/fire")
	SAKU O 0 A_CustomMissile("SakuyaKnife1",32,-256,0,CMF_AIMOFFSET)
	SAKU O 0 A_CustomMissile("SakuyaKnife1",32,256,0,CMF_AIMOFFSET)

	SAKU O 6 A_CustomMissile("SakuyaKnife1",32,0,0)

  MissileHard:
	SAKU A 0 A_ChangeFlag("FRIGHTENED",1)
	SAKU A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOPAIN",1)

  MissileEnd:
	SAKU A 0 A_TakeInventory("PowerTimeFreezer",0x7FFFFFFF)
	SAKU A 0 A_TakeInventory("SakuyaTimeFreeze",0x7FFFFFFF)
	SAKU A 0 A_TakeInventory("EnemyCounter4",600)
	SAKU A 0 A_ChangeFlag("FRIGHTENED",0)
	SAKU A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOPAIN",0)
	SAKU PQR 5 A_FaceTarget

  MissileUltra:
	SAKU A 0 A_ChangeFlag("FRIGHTENED",1)
	SAKU A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOPAIN",1)
	SAKU FGH 5 A_FaceTarget
	SAKU IIIIIIIIIIIIIIIIIIIIIIIIIIIIIIIIIIIIIIIIIIIIIIIIIIIIIIIIIIIIIIIIIIIIIIIIIIIIIIII 0 A_CustomMissile("SakuyaJackTheLudoBileOrb",32,0,frandom(90,-90),CMF_OFFSETPITCH,frandom(10,-10))

	SAKU IJKLMN 5 A_FaceTarget
	SAKU O 0 A_GiveInventory("SakuyaTimeFreeze",1) //OH GOD HERE WE GO AGAIN
	Goto HardLoop
  Death:
	SAKU S 1 ACS_NamedTerminate("BHI_BossStartAttack",0)
	SAKU S 1 ACS_NamedExecute("BHI_BossStopAttack",0)
	SAKU S 0 ACS_Execute(603)
	SAKU S 0 A_GiveInventory("BulletDeathTrigger",1)
	SAKU S 0 A_NoBlocking
    SAKU S 0 A_Scream
	SAKU SSSSSSSSSS 1 A_FadeOut(0.1)
    Stop
  }
}
ACTOR SakuyaClockCorpseOrb : FairyMaidShot4
{
	Speed 20
	FastSpeed 25
}
ACTOR SakuyaJackTheLudoBileOrb
{
  Speed 25
  FastSpeed 25
  Radius 10
  Height 20
  damage (20)
  Scale 1.0
  Projectile
  +FORCEXYBILLBOARD
  RenderStyle Add
  SeeSound "touhou/fire"
  DeathSound "touhou/hit"
  States
  {
  Spawn:
	RBUB A 0 Bright
	RBUB A 0 Bright A_ScaleVelocity(frandom(0.2,1.8))
  LoopState:
    RBUB A 1 Bright A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("BulletDeathTrigger",1,"Death")
    Loop
  Death:
    RBUB AAAAAAAAAA 1 Bright A_FadeOut
    Stop
  }
}

ACTOR SakuyaWorldOrb1
{
  Radius 8
  Height 16
  Speed 12
  FastSpeed 18
  damage (16)
  Scale 0.75
  Projectile
  +FORCEXYBILLBOARD
  RenderStyle Add
  SeeSound "touhou/fire"
  DeathSound "touhou/hit"
  States
  {
  Spawn:
    MANF ABABABAB 4 Bright A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("BulletDeathTrigger",1,"Death")
	MANF B 0 Bright A_Stop
	MANF B 0 Bright A_SetAngle(angle+frandom(-90,90))
	MANF B 0 Bright ThrustThing(angle*256/360,15,1,0)
	Goto SpawnLoop
  SpawnLoop:
	MANF AAAABBBB 1 Bright A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("BulletDeathTrigger",1,"Death")
    Loop
  Death:
    MISL CDE 8 Bright
    Stop
  }
}

ACTOR SakuyaNS3Knife1 : SakuyaKnife1
{
	Speed 12
	FastSpeed 20
	+HEXENBOUNCE
	BounceCount 3
	States
	{
	Spawn:
		KNIF A 1 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("BulletDeathTrigger",1,"Death")
		Loop
	}
}

	BounceCount 3
	States
	{
	Spawn:
		KNF2 A 1 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("BulletDeathTrigger",1,"Death")
		Loop
	}
}

ACTOR SakuyaKillingDoll
{
//$Category "Touhou Characters"
  Tag "Sakuya Izayoi"
  floatspeed 10
  Speed 10
  fastspeed 12
  MONSTER
  Health 2250
  Radius 24
  Height 64
  Scale 0.7
  MinMissileChance 32
  Mass 7000
  Species SDM
  +MISSILEMORE
  +MISSILEEVENMORE
  +INVULNERABLE
  +NOPAIN
  +DONTHURTSPECIES
  +AVOIDMELEE
  +LOOKALLAROUND
  +FLOORCLIP
  +NOICEDEATH
  +NOTIMEFREEZE
  +DONTFALL
  +DONTRIP
  +DONTMORPH
  +NORADIUSDMG
  +AMBUSH

  Painchance 4
  Painsound "touhou/pain"
  Deathsound "touhou/defeat"
  Obituary "%o was knived by Sakuya."

  {
  Spawn:
	SAKU A 0
	SAKU A 15 A_SetTranslucent(0.1,0)
	SAKU AAAAAAAAAA 2 A_FadeIn(0.1)
  Idle:
	SAKU A 3 A_Look
    Loop
  See:
    SAKU A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("SpellcardActive",1,"ChaseState")
    SAKU A 0 A_GiveInventory("SpellcardActive",1)
	SAKU B 6 A_FaceTarget
    TNT1 A 0 Thing_ChangeTID(0,6040)
    TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecute("BHI_BossStartAttack",0,6040,0,true)
	TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecute("BHI_BossStartTimer",0,6040,60)
	SAKU B 0 ACS_Execute(602,0,24)
	SAKU B 0 A_PlaySound("touhou/spellcard",0,1,0,ATTN_NONE)
	SAKU CDEDE 6 A_FaceTarget
	SAKU A 0 A_UnSetInvulnerable
	SAKU A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOPAIN",0)
	Goto Missile
  ChaseState:
	SAKU A 0 A_UnSetInvulnerable
	SAKU A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOPAIN",0)
    SAKU A 3 A_Chase
	SAKU A 0 A_TakeInventory("EnemyCounter3",1)
	SAKU A 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("UltraMode",1,"TakeAllAmmo")
    Loop
  TakeAllAmmo:
	SAKU A 0 A_TakeInventory("EnemyCounter3",50)
    Goto ChaseState
  Pain:
    SAKU S 5 A_Pain
    Goto See
  Melee:
  Missile:

	SAKU A 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("NormalMode",1,"MissileNormal")
	SAKU A 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("HardMode",1,"MissileHard")
	SAKU A 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("LunaticMode",1,"MissileLunatic")
	Goto MissileHard
  MissileEasy:

	SAKU P 0 A_CustomMissile("SakuyaKillingDollKnife1",32,0,6,CMF_AIMDIRECTION)

	SAKU P 0 A_CustomMissile("SakuyaKillingDollKnife2",32,0,-8,CMF_AIMDIRECTION)
	SAKU P 0 A_CustomMissile("SakuyaKillingDollKnife2",32,0,8,CMF_AIMDIRECTION)
	SAKU P 0 A_CustomMissile("SakuyaKillingDollKnife2",32,0,-4,CMF_AIMDIRECTION)
	SAKU P 0 A_CustomMissile("SakuyaKillingDollKnife2",32,0,4,CMF_AIMDIRECTION)

	-ACTIVATEPCROSS
	+NOTIMEFREEZE
	SeeSound "touhou/fire"
	DeathSound "touhou/hit"
	States
	{
	Spawn:
		KNIF A 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("BulletDeathTrigger",1,"Death")
		KNIF A 1 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("PowerTimeFreezer",1,"Freeze")
		Loop
	Freeze:
		KNIF A 18 A_Stop
		KNIF A 0 A_Jump(64,"Restart")
		KNF3 A 18 A_SetAngle(frandom(0,360))
		KNF3 A 0 ThrustThing(angle*256/360,16,1,0)
		Goto LoopState
	LoopState:
		KNF3 A 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("BulletDeathTrigger",1,"Death")
		KNF3 A 1 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("PowerTimeFreezer",1,"Freeze2")
		Loop
	Freeze2:
		KNF3 A 35 A_Stop
		KNF3 A 0 ThrustThing(angle*256/360,16,1,0)
		Goto LoopState
	Restart:
		KNIF A 20
		KNIF A 0 ThrustThing(angle*256/360,12,1,0)
		Goto Spawn
	Death:
		KNIF AAAAAAAAAA 1 A_FadeOut(0.1)
		Stop
	}
}

{
    Speed 10
	FastSpeed 12
	States

		Goto LoopState
	Restart:
		KNF2 A 18
		KNF2 A 0 ThrustThing(angle*256/360,12,1,0)
		Goto Spawn
	}
}
